This page is really javascript heavy. Give it a few seconds to load!! I've only tested in Chrome, so hopefully it works in other browsers.

Notable Column Definitions:
  • Inj - Injury status. Red - Questionable/Doubtful. Yellow - Probable. Green - No Injury.
  • 3 Years - Sparkline for last 3 years of fantasy performance.
  • Defensive Opp - "Defensive opportunity" - ie I ranked opposing defenses by their average points against. Red indicates good teams blue is bad teams - you want more blue. More about this on my blog
  • Draft Distribution - Distribution of draft picks in 24,000 mock drafts that I scraped from some mock draft site. It looks normally distributed for most players, centered around the "Mock Draft Avg" column
  • ESPN/CBS/ADP - Espn, CBS, and Average Draft Position rankings (which is a mean of the rankings from a bunch of different sources)
If you click a row, it'll turn black - so you can use this in drafts
